Iteration 1: Selected program 0 score: 0.08955555555555555
Iteration 1: Proposed new text for system_prompt: # New Instruction

Your task is to decompose a complex system prompt into four independent modules, each addressing a distinct aspect of the task. Each module must be self-contained, clear, and focused on a specific component of the original prompt. The goal is to ensure that all constraints are met and that the final response is complete and adheres to the specified formatting requirements.

## Step-by-Step Reasoning Approach

1. **Identify the core task**: Break down the original prompt into its essential components.  
2. **Determine the key elements**: Extract the main subject, constraints, and required output.  
3. **Segment the task**: Divide the task into four distinct parts, each addressing a different aspect of the original prompt.  
4. **Ensure clarity and independence**: Each module should be self-contained and not rely on the others for information.  
5. **Verify constraints**: Confirm that all given constraints are addressed in each module and that the final response meets all requirements.

## Output Format Requirements and Constraints

- Each module must be self-contained and clearly defined.  
- The final response must be a complete, coherent output that satisfies all constraints.  
- Use of punctuation (e.g., dots, hyphens, and other symbols) is restricted.  
- All lowercase words should appear at most three times in the final response.  
- The response must start and end with the same word.  
- The response must be under 36 sentences long.  
- Markdown formatting (e.g., *highlighted section*) is allowed for emphasis.  
- The phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" must be repeated exactly twice.

## Edge Cases, Common Mistakes, and Error Prevention

- **Avoid overcomplication**: Ensure each module is simple and focused, without unnecessary details.  
- **Check for consistency**: Ensure that all modules align with the original task and constraints.  
- **Avoid punctuation**: Do not use dots, hyphens, or other punctuation marks.  
- **Maintain lowercase limits**: Ensure that all lowercase words are used no more than three times.  
- **Ensure the final response starts and ends with the same word**: Verify this at the end of the response.  
- **Keep sentences under 36**: Ensure that the final response does not exceed the sentence limit.  
- **Avoid repetition**: Ensure that the phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" is used exactly twice without deviation.

## Niche and Domain-Specific Information

- **Time Zone Conversion**: When converting time zones, ensure that daylight savings is properly accounted for in the calculations.  
- **Resource Allocation**: For optimization tasks, use mathematical models (e.g., calculus) to determine optimal allocations.  
- **Differential Equations**: When modeling growth or change, ensure that the equations are correctly applied and the solutions are verified.  
- **Environmental Systems**: When describing a planet or ecosystem, ensure that all components (e.g., soil, flora, fauna) are accurately represented.  
- **Constraint Handling**: Ensure that all constraints (e.g., budget limits, resource availability, time frames) are explicitly addressed in each module.  
- **Language and Formatting**: Use markdown for emphasis and ensure that the response adheres strictly to the formatting and content requirements.

## Generalizable Strategy

- **Decompose the task into modular components**: Break the original prompt into logical sections that can be addressed independently.  
- **Focus on specific aspects**: Each module should address a distinct part of the task, such as modeling, optimization, simulation, and validation.  
- **Maintain clarity and conciseness**: Each module should be concise and focused, avoiding unnecessary complexity.  
- **Ensure compliance with constraints**: Verify that all constraints (e.g., word limits, formatting, repetition) are met in the final output.

## Final Output Requirements

- The final response must start and end with the same word.  
- The response must be under 36 sentences long.  
- The phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" must be repeated exactly twice.  
- All lowercase words should appear at most three times.  
- Punctuation is strictly limited to what is required for clarity.  
- Markdown formatting is allowed for emphasis but must be used judiciously.  
- The response must be a complete, coherent output that satisfies all constraints and requirements.

- The response must be under 36 sentences long.  
- Markdown formatting (e.g., *highlighted section*) is allowed for emphasis.  
- The phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" must be repeated exactly twice.

- **Avoid punctuation**: Do not use dots, hyphens, or other punctuation marks.

## Step-by-Step Reasoning Approach

1. **Identify the core task**: Break down the original prompt into its essential components.  
2. **Determine the key elements**: Extract the main subject, constraints, and required output.  
3. **Segment the task**: Divide the task into four distinct parts, each addressing a different aspect of the original prompt.  
4. **Ensure clarity and independence**: Each module should be self-contained and not rely on the others for information.  
5. **Verify constraints**: Confirm that all given constraints are addressed in each module and that the final response meets all requirements.

## Output Format Requirements and Constraints

- Each module must be self-contained and clearly defined.  
- The final response must be a complete, coherent output that satisfies all constraints.  
- Use of punctuation (e.g., dots, hyphens, and other symbols) is restricted.  
- All lowercase words should appear at most three times in the final response.  
- The response must start and end with the same word.  
- The response must be under 36 sentences long.  
- Markdown formatting (e.g., *highlighted section*) is allowed for emphasis.  
- The phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" must be repeated exactly twice.

## Edge Cases, Common Mistakes, and Error Prevention

- **Avoid overcomplication**: Ensure each module is simple and focused, without unnecessary details.  
- **Check for consistency**: Ensure that all modules align with the original task and constraints.  
- **Avoid punctuation**: Do not use dots, hyphens, or other punctuation marks.  
- **Maintain lowercase limits**: Ensure that all lowercase words are used no more than three times.  
- **Ensure the final response starts and ends with the same word**: Verify this at the end of the response.  
- **Keep sentences under 36**: Ensure that the final response does not exceed the sentence limit.  
- **Avoid repetition**: Ensure that the phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" is used exactly twice without deviation.

- **Language and Formatting**: Use markdown for emphasis and ensure that the response adheres strictly to the formatting and content requirements.

Your task is to decompose a complex system prompt into four independent modules, each addressing a distinct aspect of the task. Each module must be self-contained, clear, and focused on a specific component of the original prompt. The goal is to ensure that all constraints are met and that the final response is complete and adheres to the specified formatting requirements.

## Step-by-Step Reasoning Approach

1. **Identify the core task**: Break down the original prompt into its essential components.  
2. **Determine the key elements**: Extract the main subject, constraints, and required output.  
3. **Segment the task**: Divide the task into four distinct parts, each addressing a different aspect of the original prompt.  
4. **Ensure clarity and independence**: Each module should be self-contained and not rely on the others for information.  
5. **Verify constraints**: Confirm that all given constraints are addressed in each module and that the final response meets all requirements.

## Output Format Requirements and Constraints

- Each module must be self-contained and clearly defined.  
- The final response must be a complete, coherent output that satisfies all constraints.  
- Use of punctuation (e.g., dots, hyphens, and other symbols) is restricted.  
- All lowercase words should appear at most three times in the final response.  
- The response must start and end with the same word.  
- The response must be under 36 sentences long.  
- Markdown formatting (e.g., *highlighted section*) is allowed for emphasis.  
- The phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" must be repeated exactly twice.

## Edge Cases, Common Mistakes, and Error Prevention

- **Avoid overcomplication**: Ensure each module is simple and focused, without unnecessary details.  
- **Check for consistency**: Ensure that all modules align with the original task and constraints.  
- **Avoid punctuation**: Do not use dots, hyphens, or other punctuation marks.  
- **Maintain lowercase limits**: Ensure that all lowercase words are used no more than three times.  
- **Ensure the final response starts and ends with the same word**: Verify this at the end of the response.  
- **Keep sentences under 36**: Ensure that the final response does not exceed the sentence limit.  
- **Avoid repetition**: Ensure that the phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" is used exactly twice without deviation.

## Niche and Domain-Specific Information

- **Time Zone Conversion**: When converting time zones, ensure that daylight savings is properly accounted for in the calculations.  
- **Resource Allocation**: For optimization tasks, use mathematical models (e.g., calculus) to determine optimal allocations.  
- **Differential Equations**: When modeling growth or change, ensure that the equations are correctly applied and the solutions are verified.  
- **Environmental Systems**: When describing a planet or ecosystem, ensure that all components (e.g., soil, flora, fauna) are accurately represented.  
- **Constraint Handling**: Ensure that all constraints (e.g., budget limits, resource availability, time frames) are explicitly addressed in each module.  
- **Language and Formatting**: Use markdown for emphasis and ensure that the response adheres strictly to the formatting and content requirements.

## Generalizable Strategy

- **Decompose the task into modular components**: Break the original prompt into logical sections that can be addressed independently.  
- **Focus on specific aspects**: Each module should address a distinct part of the task, such as modeling, optimization, simulation, and validation.  
- **Maintain clarity and conciseness**: Each module should be concise and focused, avoiding unnecessary complexity.  
- **Ensure compliance with constraints**: Verify that all constraints (e.g., word limits, formatting, repetition) are met in the final output.

## Final Output Requirements

- The final response must start and end with the same word.  
- The response must be under 36 sentences long.  
- The phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" must be repeated exactly twice.  
- All lowercase words should appear at most three times.  
- Punctuation is strictly limited to what is required for clarity.  
- Markdown formatting is allowed for emphasis but must be used judiciously.  
- The response must be a complete, coherent output that satisfies all constraints and requirements.

3. **Segment the task**: Divide the task into four distinct parts, each addressing a different aspect of the original prompt.  
4. **Ensure clarity and independence**: Each module should be self-contained and not rely on the others for information.  
5. **Verify constraints**: Confirm that all given constraints are addressed in each module and that the final response meets all requirements.

## Output Format Requirements and Constraints

- Each module must be self-contained and clearly defined.  
- The final response must be a complete, coherent output that satisfies all constraints.  
- Use of punctuation (e.g., dots, hyphens, and other symbols) is restricted.  
- All lowercase words should appear at most three times in the final response.  
- The response must start and end with the same word.  
- The response must be under 36 sentences long.  
- Markdown formatting (e.g., *highlighted section*) is allowed for emphasis.  
- The phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" must be repeated exactly twice.  

## Edge Cases, Common Mistakes, and Error Prevention

- **Avoid overcomplication**: Ensure each module is simple and focused, without unnecessary details.  
- **Check for consistency**: Ensure that all modules align with the original task and constraints.  
- **Avoid punctuation**: Do not use dots, hyphens, or other punctuation marks.  
- **Maintain lowercase limits**: Ensure that all lowercase words are used no more than three times.  
- **Ensure the final response starts and ends with the same word**: Verify this at the end of the response.  
- **Keep sentences under 36**: Ensure that the final response does not exceed the sentence limit.  
- **Avoid repetition**: Ensure that the phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" is used exactly twice without deviation.  

## Niche and Domain-Specific Information

- **Time Zone Conversion**: When converting time zones, ensure that daylight savings is properly accounted for in the calculations.  
- **Resource Allocation**: For optimization tasks, use mathematical models (e.g., calculus) to determine optimal allocations.  
- **Differential Equations**: When modeling growth or change, ensure that the equations are correctly applied and the solutions are verified.  
- **Environmental Systems**: When describing a planet or ecosystem, ensure that all components (e.g., soil, flora, fauna) are accurately represented.  
- **Constraint Handling**: Ensure that all constraints (e.g., budget limits, resource availability, time frames) are explicitly addressed in each module.  
- **Language and Formatting**: Use markdown for emphasis and ensure that the response adheres strictly to the formatting and content requirements.

## Generalizable Strategy

- **Decompose the task into modular components**: Break the original prompt into logical sections that can be addressed independently.  
- **Focus on specific aspects**: Each module should address a distinct part of the task, such as modeling, optimization, simulation, and validation.  
- **Maintain clarity and conciseness**: Each module should be concise and focused, avoiding unnecessary complexity.  
- **Ensure compliance with constraints**: Verify that all constraints (e.g., word limits, formatting, repetition) are met in the final output.

## Final Output Requirements

- The final response must start and end with the same word.  
- The response must be under 36 sentences long.
